href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#everything-below-this-point-will-happen-at-query-time" class="break-words py-1 block border-l pl-4 border-gray-950/5 dark:border-white/10 hover:border-gray-950/20 dark:hover:border-white/20 hover:text-gray-900 dark:text-gray-400 dark:hover:text-gray-300">Everything below this point will happen at query time!</a></li><li class="toc-item relative" data-depth="0"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#reranker-to-improve-quality" class="break-words py-1 Quality</a></li><li class="toc-item relative" data-depth="0"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#call-generative-model-llama-3-1-405b" [contain:inline-size] isolate empty:hidden mb-14" data-page-title="Implement contextual RAG from Anthropic" data-page-href="/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic" id="content"><blockquote class="sr-only" data-agent-docs-index="true"><h2>Documentation Index</h2><p>Fetch the complete documentation index at: <a href="https://docs.together.ai/llms.txt">https://docs.together.ai/llms.txt</a></p><p>Use this file to discover all available pages before exploring further.</p></blockquote><span data-as="p"><a href="https://www.anthropic.com/news/contextual-retrieval" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Contextual Retrieval</a> is a chunk augmentation technique that uses an LLM to enhance each chunk.</span>
<div><div data-name="frame" class="frame p-2 not-prose relative bg-gray-50/50 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden dark:bg-gray-800/25 print:print-color-exact"><div style="background-position:10px 10px" dark:[mask-image:linear-gradient(0deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.1),rgba(255,255,255,0.5))] print:print-color-exact"></div><div class="relative rounded-xl overflow-hidden flex justify-center"><span aria-owns="rmiz-modal-" data-rmiz=""><span data-rmiz-content="not-found" style="visibility:visible"><picture class="contents"><img data-path="images/guides/11.png" src="https://mintcdn.com/togetherai-52386018/msWWavplJrEZR36N/images/guides/11.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=msWWavplJrEZR36N&q=85&s=c95e14ec01de84f03a0982ea44d565c4" alt="" class="object-contain" width="3840" height="2160" decoding="async" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 576px" srcSet="https://mintcdn.com/togetherai-52386018/msWWavplJrEZR36N/images/guides/11.png?w=280&fit=max&auto=format&n=msWWavplJrEZR36N&q=85&s=d51f62f41d26706932895aa10cdb0fda 280w, <span data-as="p">Here’s an overview of how it works.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="contextual-rag"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#contextual-rag" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Contextual RAG:</span></h2>
<ol>
<li>For every chunk - prepend an explanatory context snippet that situates the chunk within the rest of the document. -&gt; Get a small cost effective LLM to do this.</li>
<li>Hybrid Search: Embed the chunk using both sparse (keyword) and dense(semantic) embeddings.</li>
<li>Perform rank fusion using an algorithm like Reciprocal Rank Fusion(RRF).</li>
<li>Retrieve top 150 chunks and pass those to a Reranker to obtain top 20 chunks.</li>
<li>Pass top 20 chunks to LLM to generate an answer.</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p">Below we implement each step in this process using Open Source models.</span>
<span data-as="p">To breakdown the concept further we break down the process into a one-time indexing step and a query time step.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Data Ingestion Phase:</strong></span>
<div><div data-name="frame" class="frame p-2 not-prose relative bg-gray-50/50 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden dark:bg-gray-800/25 print:print-color-exact"><div style="background-position:10px 10px" class="absolute inset-0 bg-grid-neutral-200/20 [mask-image:linear-gradient(0deg,#fff,rgba(255,255,255,0.6))] dark:bg-grid-white/5 dark:[mask-image:linear-gradient(0deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.1),rgba(255,255,255,0.5))] print:print-color-exact"></div><div class="relative rounded-xl overflow-hidden flex justify-center"><span aria-owns="rmiz-modal-" data-rmiz=""><span data-rmiz-content="not-found" style="visibility:visible"><picture class="contents"><img data-path="images/guides/12.png" src="https://mintcdn.com/togetherai-52386018/msWWavplJrEZR36N/images/guides/12.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=msWWavplJrEZR36N&q=85&s=3d2da83adbb003deca81154f23d11867" alt="" class="object-contain" srcSet="https://mintcdn.com/togetherai-52386018/msWWavplJrEZR36N/images/guides/12.png?w=280&fit=max&auto=format&n=msWWavplJrEZR36N&q=85&s=c93703cef1766f91b2b0f18d21801fc1 280w, <li>Data processing and chunking</li>
<li>Context generation using Qwen3.5-9B</li>
<li>Vector Embedding and Index Generation</li>
<li>BM25 Keyword Index Generation</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p"><strong>At Query Time:</strong></span>
<div><div data-name="frame" class="frame p-2 not-prose relative bg-gray-50/50 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden dark:bg-gray-800/25 print:print-color-exact"><div style="background-position:10px 10px" aria-owns="rmiz-modal-" data-rmiz=""><span data-rmiz-content="not-found" style="visibility:visible"><picture class="contents"><img data-path="images/guides/13.png" <ol>
<li>Perform retrieval using both indices and combine them using RRF</li>
<li>Reranker to improve retrieval quality</li>

<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="install-libraries"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#install-libraries" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Install Libraries</span></h2>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 code-block-background [&_*]:ring-0 [&_*]:outline-0 [&_*]:focus:ring-0 [&_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-xt bg-white overflow-x-auto scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-rounded scrollbar-thumb-black/15 data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="python"><code language="python" numberOfLines="37"><span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># Let's download the essay from Paul Graham's website</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">import</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> requests</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">from</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> bs4 </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">import</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> BeautifulSoup</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> scrape_pg_essay</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">():</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    url </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> "https://paulgraham.com/foundermode.html"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    try</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">        # Send GET request to the URL</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        response </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> requests.get(url)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        response.raise_for_status()  </span><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># Raise an error for bad status codes</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">        # Parse the HTML content</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        soup </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> BeautifulSoup(response.text, </span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"html.parser"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">        # Paul Graham's essays typically have the main content in a font tag</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">        # You might need to adjust this selector based on the actual HTML structure</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        content </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> soup.find(</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"font"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">        if</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> content:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">            # Extract and clean the text</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">            text </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> content.get_text()</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">            # Remove extra whitespace and normalize line breaks</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">            text </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> " "</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">.join(text.split())</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">            return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> text</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">        else</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">            return</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> "Could not find the main content of the essay."</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    except</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> requests.RequestException </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">as</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> e:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">        return</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6"> f</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"Error fetching the webpage: </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">{</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">e</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">}</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># Scrape the essay</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">pg_essay </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> scrape_pg_essay()</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">This will give us the essay, we still need to chunk the essay, so let’s implement a function and use it:</span>

class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="python"><code language="python" numberOfLines="14"><span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># We can get away with naive fixed sized chunking as the context generation will add meaning to these chunks</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> create_chunks</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">document</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">chunk_size</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">300</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">overlap</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">50</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        document[i : i </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">+</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> chunk_size]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">        for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> i </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> range</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">len</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(document), chunk_size </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">-</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> overlap)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    ]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">chunks </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> create_chunks(pg_essay, </span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">chunk_size</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">250</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">overlap</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">30</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> i, chunk </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> enumerate</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(chunks):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">    print</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">f</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"Chunk </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">{</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">i </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">+</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 1</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">}</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">: </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">{</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">chunk</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">}</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>

<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="generating-contextual-chunks"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#generating-contextual-chunks" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Generating Contextual Chunks</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">This part contains the main intuition behind <code>Contextual Retrieval</code>. We will make an LLM call for each chunk to add much needed relevant context to the chunk. In order to do this we pass in the ENTIRE document per LLM call.</span>
<span data-as="p">It may seem that passing in the entire document per chunk and making an LLM call per chunk is quite inefficient, this is true and there very well might be more efficient techniques to accomplish the same end goal. But in keeping with implementing the current technique at hand let’s do it.</span>
<span data-as="p">Additionally using quantized small 1-3B models (here we will use Llama 3.2 3B) along with prompt caching does make this more feasible.</span>
<span data-as="p">Prompt caching allows key and value matrices corresponding to the document to be cached for future LLM calls.</span>
<span data-as="p">We will use the following prompt to generate context for each chunk:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/5 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark p-0.5" numberOfLines="14" language="python"><div class="flex text-gray-400 text-xs rounded-t-[14px] leading-6 font-medium pl-4 pr-2.5 py-1" data-component-part="code-block-header"><div class="flex-grow-0 flex items-center gap-1.5 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 min-w-0" data-component-part="code-block-header-filename"><span class="truncate min-w-0" title="Python">Python</span></div><div class="flex-1 flex items-center justify-end gap-1.5 print:hidden"><div class="z-10 select-none" data-state="closed"><button class="h-[26px] w-[26px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-md backdrop-blur group/copy-button" data-testid="copy-code-button" aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg width="18" dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 14.25V7.25C16.25 6.14543 15.3546 5.25 14.25 5.25Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" /><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 numberOfLines="14"><span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># We want to generate a snippet explaining the relevance/importance of the chunk with</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># full document in mind.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">CONTEXTUAL_RAG_PROMPT</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> =</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> """</span></span>

<span class="line"></span>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">Answer ONLY with a succinct explaination of the meaning of the chunk in the context of the whole document above.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"""</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Now we can prep each chunk into these prompt template and generate the context:</span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">from</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> together </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">import</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> Together</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># Paste in your Together AI API Key or load it</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">TOGETHER_API_KEY</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> =</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> os.environ.get(</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"TOGETHER_API_KEY"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">client </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> Together(</span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">api_key</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">TOGETHER_API_KEY</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># First we will just generate the prompts and examine them</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> generate_prompts</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">document</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">chunks</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]) -&gt; List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    prompts </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> []</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> chunk </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> chunks:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        prompt </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> CONTEXTUAL_RAG_PROMPT</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">.format(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">            WHOLE_DOCUMENT</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">document,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">            CHUNK_CONTENT</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">chunk,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        prompts.append(prompt)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> prompts</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">prompts </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> generate_prompts(pg_essay, chunks)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> generate_context</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">prompt</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Generates a contextual response based on the given prompt using the specified language model.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Args:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        prompt (str): The input prompt to generate a response for.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Returns:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        str: The generated response content from the language model.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    response </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> client.chat.completions.create(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">        model</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"Qwen/Qwen3.5-9B"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">        messages</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">[{</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"role"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"user"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"content"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: prompt}],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">        temperature</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">1</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> response.choices[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">].message.content</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">We can now use the functions above to generate context for each chunk and append it to the chunk itself:</span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">contextual_chunks </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> [</span></span>

<span data-as="p">Now we can embed each chunk into a vector index.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="vector-index"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#vector-index" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Vector Index</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">We will now use <code>multilingual-e5-large-instruct</code> to embed the augmented chunks above into a vector index.</span>

<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> generate_embeddings</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    input_texts</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">],</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    model_api_string</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">) -&gt; List[List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">float</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]]:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """Generate embeddings from Together python library.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Args:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        input_texts: a list of string input texts.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        model_api_string: str. An API string for a specific embedding model of your choice.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Returns:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        embeddings_list: a list of embeddings. Each element corresponds to the each input text.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    outputs </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> client.embeddings.create(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">        input</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">input_texts,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">        model</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">model_api_string,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    )</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> [x.embedding </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> x </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> outputs.data]</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">contextual_embeddings </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> generate_embeddings(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    contextual_chunks,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    "intfloat/multilingual-e5-large-instruct"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Next we need to write a function that can retrieve the top matching chunks from this index given a query:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/5 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="python"><code language="python" numberOfLines="28"><span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> vector_retrieval</span><span <span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    query</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">str</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    top_k</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">int</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> =</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 5</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    vector_index</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: np.ndarray </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6"> None</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">) -&gt; List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">int</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Retrieve the top-k most similar items from an index based on a query.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Args:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        query (str): The query string to search for.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        top_k (int, optional): The number of top similar items to retrieve. Defaults to 5.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        index (np.ndarray, optional): The index array containing embeddings to search against. Defaults to None.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Returns:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        List[int]: A list of indices corresponding to the top-k most similar items in the index.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    query_embedding </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> generate_embeddings(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">        [query], </span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"intfloat/multilingual-e5-large-instruct"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    )[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    similarity_scores </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> cosine_similarity([query_embedding], vector_index)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> list</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(np.argsort(</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">-</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">similarity_scores)[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">][:top_k])</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">vector_retreival(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    query</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"What are 'skip-level' meetings?"</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    top_k</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">5</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    vector_index</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">contextual_embeddings,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">We now have a way to retrieve from the vector index given a query.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="bm25-index"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#bm25-index" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">BM25 Index</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Let’s build a keyword index that allows us to use BM25 to perform lexical search based on the words present in the query and the contextual chunks. For this we will use the <code>bm25s</code> python library:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/5 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border <span data-as="p">Which can be queried as follows:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/5 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border <span data-as="p">Similar to the function above which produces vector results from the vector index we can write a function that produces keyword search results from the BM25 index:</span>

numberOfLines="14"><span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> bm25_retrieval</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">bm25_index</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">) -&gt; List[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">int</span><span <span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Retrieve the top-k document indices based on the BM25 algorithm for a given query.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Args:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">        query (str): The search query string.</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    results, scores </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> bm25_index.retrieve(bm25s.tokenize(query), </span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">k</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">k)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> [contextual_chunks.index(doc) </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> doc </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> results[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">]]</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="everything-below-this-point-will-happen-at-query-time"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#everything-below-this-point-will-happen-at-query-time" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Everything below this point will happen at query time!</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Once a user submits a query we are going to use both functions above to perform Vector and BM25 retrieval and then fuse the ranks using the RRF algorithm implemented below.</span>

<span data-as="p">The Reciprocal Rank Fusion algorithm takes two ranked list of objects and combines them:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group min-w-0 print:print-color-exact text-gray-950 bg-gray-50 dark:bg-white/5 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border data-component-part="code-block-header"><div class="flex-grow-0 flex items-center gap-1.5 text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 min-w-0" data-component-part="code-block-header-filename"><span class="truncate min-w-0" title="Python">Python</span></div><div class="flex-1 flex items-center justify-end gap-1.5 print:hidden"><div class="z-10 select-none" data-state="closed"><button class="h-[26px] w-[26px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-md backdrop-blur group/copy-button" data-testid="copy-code-button" aria-label="Copy the contents from the code block"><svg width="18" dark:group-hover/copy-button:text-white/60"><path d="M14.25 5.25H7.25C6.14543 5.25 5.25 6.14543 5.25 7.25V14.25C5.25 15.3546 6.14543 16.25 7.25 16.25H14.25C15.3546 16.25 16.25 15.3546 16.25 14.25V7.25C16.25 6.14543 15.3546 5.25 14.25 5.25Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" /><path d="M2.80103 11.998L1.77203 5.07397C1.61003 3.98097 /></svg></button></div><div class="z-10 select-none" data-state="closed"><button class="h-[26px] w-[26px] flex items-center justify-center rounded-md backdrop-blur group/ask-assistant-button" code-block-background [&_*]:ring-0 [&_*]:outline-0 [&_*]:focus:ring-0 [&_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-xt bg-white overflow-x-auto scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-rounded scrollbar-thumb-black/15 hover:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 active:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 dark:scrollbar-thumb-white/20 dark:hover:scrollbar-thumb-white/25 dark:active:scrollbar-thumb-white/25" data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="python"><code language="python" numberOfLines="27"><span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">from</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> collections </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">import</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> defaultdict</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">def</span><span style="color:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> reciprocal_rank_fusion</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">*</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">list_of_list_ranks_system</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">, </span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">K</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">60</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Fuse rank from multiple IR systems using Reciprocal Rank Fusion.</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Args:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    * list_of_list_ranks_system: Ranked results from different IR system.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    K (int): A constant used in the RRF formula (default is 60).</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Returns:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    Tuple of list of sorted documents by score and sorted documents</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">    """</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    # Dictionary to store RRF mapping</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    rrf_map </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> defaultdict(</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">float</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    # Calculate RRF score for each result in each list</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> rank_list </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> list_of_list_ranks_system:</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">        for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> rank, item </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> enumerate</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(rank_list, </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">1</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">):</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">            rrf_map[item] </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">+=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 1</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> /</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> (rank </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">+</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> K)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    # Sort items based on their RRF scores in descending order</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">    sorted_items </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> sorted</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">(rrf_map.items(), </span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">key</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">lambda</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> x</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">: x[</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">1</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">], </span><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">reverse</span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">=</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6">True</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4">)</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    # Return tuple of list of sorted documents by score and sorted documents</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> sorted_items, [item </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">for</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> item, score </span><span style="color:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">in</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> sorted_items]</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">We can use the RRF function above as follows:</span>

<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="reranker-to-improve-quality"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="https://docs.together.ai/docs/how-to-implement-contextual-rag-from-anthropic#reranker-to-improve-quality" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z" /></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Reranker To improve Quality</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">Now we add a retrieval quality improvement step here to make sure only the highest and most semantically similar chunks get sent to our LLM.</span>
<div class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-2xl flex gap-3 border border-green-200 bg-green-50 dark:border-green-900 dark:bg-green-600/20 [&_[data-component-part='callout-icon']]:mt-px" [&_strong]:!text-current text-green-800 dark:text-green-300" data-component-part="callout-content"><span data-as="p">Rerank models like <code>Mxbai-Rerank-Large-V2</code> are only available as <a children:!bg-transparent transition-[height] duration-300 ease-in-out code-block-background [&_*]:ring-0 [&_*]:outline-0 [&_*]:focus:ring-0 [&_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-2xl bg-white overflow-x-auto dark:active:scrollbar-thumb-white/25" data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E;color:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4" language="text"><code language="text" numberOfLines="2"><span class="line"><span>'"Skip-level" meetings refer to a management practice where a CEO or high-level executive engages directly with employees who are not their direct reports, bypassing the traditional hierarchical structure of the organization. This approach is characteristic of "founder mode," where the CEO seeks to have a more direct connection with the company beyond their immediate team. In contrast to the traditional "manager mode," where decisions are made through a hierarchical system, skip-level meetings allow for more open communication and collaboration between the CEO and various levels of employees. This approach is often used by founders who want to stay connected to the company\\'s operations and culture, and to foster a more flat and collaborative organizational structure.'</span></span>
<span class="line"><span></span></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="print:hidden" data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<span data-as="p">Above we implemented Contextual Retrieval as discussed in Anthropic’s blog using fully open source models!</span>
<span data-as="p">If you want to learn more about how to best use open models refer to our <a class="link" href="https://docs.together.ai/docs">docs here</a>!</span>

a WebSocket connection for real-time text-to-speech generation. This endpoint uses WebSocket protocol (wss://api.together.ai/v1/audio/speech/websocket) for bidirectional streaming communication.\\n\\n**Connection Setup:**\\n- Protocol: WebSocket (wss://)\\n- Authentication: Pass API key as Bearer token in Authorization header\\n- Parameters: Sent as query parameters (model, voice, max_partial_length, language)\\n\\n**Client Events:**\\n- `tts_session.updated`: Update session parameters like voice. The `session` object also accepts an `extra_params` field for additional model-specific parameters that fine-tune speech generation behavior, such as `pronunciation_dict` (a list of pronunciation rules for specific characters or symbols, where each entry uses the format `\\"\\u003csource\\u003e/\\u003creplacement\\u003e\\"` (e.g., `[\\"omg/oh my god\\"]`) to override how the model pronounces matching tokens).\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"tts_session.updated\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"voice\\": \\"tara\\",\\n      \\"extra_params\\": {\\n        \\"pronunciation_dict\\": [\\"omg/oh my god\\"]\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `input_text_buffer.append`: Send text chunks for TTS generation\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"input_text_buffer.append\\",\\n    \\"text\\": \\"Hello, this is a test.\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `input_text_buffer.clear`: Clear the buffered text\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"input_text_buffer.clear\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `input_text_buffer.commit`: Signal end of text input and process remaining text\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"input_text_buffer.commit\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n\\n**Server Events:**\\n- `session.created`: Initial session confirmation (sent first)\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"event_id\\": \\"evt_123456\\",\\n    \\"type\\": \\"session.created\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"id\\": \\"session-id\\",\\n      \\"object\\": \\"realtime.tts.session\\",\\n      \\"modalities\\": [\\"text\\", \\"audio\\"],\\n      \\"model\\": \\"conversation.item.input_text.received\\",\\n    \\"text\\": \\"Hello, this is a test.\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.audio_output.delta`: Audio chunks as base64-encoded data\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.audio_output.delta\\",\\n    \\"item_id\\": \\"tts_1\\",\\n    \\"delta\\": \\"\\u003cbase64_encoded_audio_chunk\\u003e\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.audio_output.done`: Audio generation complete for an item\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.audio_output.done\\",\\n    \\"item_id\\": \\"tts_1\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.tts.failed`: Error occurred\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.tts.failed\\",\\n    \\"error\\": {\\n      \\"message\\": \\"Error description\\",\\n      \\"type\\": \\"invalid_request_error\\",\\n      \\"param\\": null,\\n      \\"code\\": \\"invalid_api_key\\"\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n\\n**Text Processing:**\\n- Partial text (no sentence ending) is held in buffer until:\\n  - We believe that the text is complete enough to be processed for TTS generation\\n  - The partial text exceeds `max_partial_length` characters (default: 250)\\n  - The `input_text_buffer.commit` event is received\\n\\n**Audio Format:**\\n- Format: Raw PCM (s16le, mono)\\n- Sample Rate: 24000 Hz\\n- Encoding: Base64 (per delta event)\\n- Delivered via `conversation.item.audio_output.delta` events\\n\\n**Error Codes:**\\n- `invalid_api_key`: Invalid API key provided (401)\\n- `missing_api_key`: Authorization header missing (401)\\n- This endpoint uses WebSocket protocol (wss://api.together.ai/v1/realtime) for bidirectional streaming communication.\\n\\n**Connection Setup:**\\n- Protocol: WebSocket (wss://)\\n- Authentication: Pass API key as Bearer token in Authorization header\\n- Parameters: Sent as query parameters (model, input_audio_format)\\n\\n**Client Events:**\\n- `input_audio_buffer.append`: Send audio chunks as base64-encoded data\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"input_audio_buffer.append\\",\\n    \\"audio\\": \\"\\u003cbase64_encoded_audio_chunk\\u003e\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `input_audio_buffer.commit`: Signal end of audio stream. When VAD is enabled, the server automatically detects speech boundaries and emits `completed` events. When VAD is disabled, you must send `commit` to trigger transcription of the buffered audio.\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"input_audio_buffer.commit\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `transcription_session.updated`: Update session configuration, including Voice Activity Detection (VAD) parameters. Send this after receiving `session.created`. Can also be sent at any time during the session to change VAD settings.\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"transcription_session.updated\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"turn_detection\\": {\\n        \\"type\\": \\"server_vad\\",\\n        \\"threshold\\": 0.3,\\n        \\"min_silence_duration_ms\\": 500,\\n        \\"min_speech_duration_ms\\": 250,\\n        \\"max_speech_duration_s\\": 5.0,\\n        \\"speech_pad_ms\\": 250\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n  To disable VAD entirely (manual commit mode), set `turn_detection` to `null`:\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"transcription_session.updated\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"turn_detection\\": null\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n\\n**Voice Activity Detection (VAD)**\\n\\nVAD controls how the server automatically detects speech segments in the audio stream. When enabled (the default), the server uses Silero VAD to identify speech regions and emits transcription events as each segment completes. When disabled, you must manually call `input_audio_buffer.commit` to trigger transcription.\\n\\nVAD can be configured in two ways:\\n1. **Query parameters** at connection time: `turn_detection=server_vad\\u0026threshold=0.3\\u0026min_silence_duration_ms=500`\\n2. **Session message** after connection: Send `transcription_session.updated` with a `turn_detection` object (see above)\\n\\nTo disable VAD at connection time, use `turn_detection=none` as a query parameter.\\n\\n**VAD Parameters:**\\n\\nAll parameters are optional. Omitted fields use their defaults.\\n\\n| Parameter | Type | Default | Description |\\n|-----------|------|---------|-------------|\\n| `type` | string | `server_vad` | VAD mode. Use `server_vad` to enable, or set `turn_detection` to `null` to disable. |\\n| `threshold` | float | `0.3` | Speech probability threshold (0.0–1.0). Audio frames with probability above this value are classified as speech. Lower values detect more speech but may increase false positives. For low-SNR audio (e.g., 8kHz phone calls), values of 0.01–0.2 may work better. |\\n| `min_silence_duration_ms` | int | `500` | Minimum silence duration in milliseconds before ending a speech segment. Higher values merge nearby speech bursts into single segments. For phone calls with mid-sentence pauses, 2000–5000ms prevents over-segmentation. |\\n| `min_speech_duration_ms` | int | `250` | Minimum speech segment duration in milliseconds. Segments shorter than this are discarded. Filters out brief noise bursts or clicks. |\\n| `max_speech_duration_s` | float | `5.0` | Maximum speech segment duration in seconds. Segments longer than this are force-split at the longest internal silence gap. Useful for continuous speech without natural pauses. |\\n| `speech_pad_ms` | int | `250` | Padding in milliseconds added to the start and end of each detected segment. Prevents clipping speech edges. When padding would cause adjacent segments to overlap, the gap is split at the midpoint instead. |\\n\\n**Server Events:**\\n- `session.created`: Initial session confirmation (sent first)\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"session.created\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"id\\": \\"session-id\\",\\n      \\"object\\": \\"realtime.session\\",\\n      \\"modalities\\": [\\"audio\\"],\\n      \\"model\\": \\"openai/whisper-large-v3\\"\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `transcription_session.updated`: Confirms session configuration was applied. Sent in response to a client `transcription_session.updated` message.\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"transcription_session.updated\\",\\n    \\"session\\": {\\n      \\"turn_detection\\": {\\n        \\"type\\": \\"server_vad\\",\\n        \\"threshold\\": 0.3,\\n        \\"min_silence_duration_ms\\": 500,\\n        \\"min_speech_duration_ms\\": 250,\\n        \\"max_speech_duration_s\\": 5.0,\\n        \\"speech_pad_ms\\": 250\\n      }\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.delta`: Partial transcription results\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.delta\\",\\n    \\"delta\\": \\"The quick brown\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.completed`: Final transcription\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.completed\\",\\n    \\"transcript\\": \\"The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog\\"\\n  }\\n  ```\\n- `conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.failed`: Error occurred\\n  ```json\\n  {\\n    \\"type\\": \\"conversation.item.input_audio_transcription.failed\\",\\n    \\"error\\": {\\n      \\"message\\": \\"Error description\\",\\n      \\"type\\": \\"invalid_request_error\\",\\n      \\"param\\": null,\\n      \\"code\\": \\"invalid_api_key\\"\\n    }\\n  }\\n  ```\\n\\n**Error Codes:**\\n- `invalid_api_key`: Invalid API key provided (401)\\n- `missing_api_key`: Authorization header missing (401)\\n- `model_not_available`: Invalid or unavailable model (400)\\n- Unsupported
